<h2 id=3D"BCPApp:DoseRounds-I:[BCPApp]DoseRounds">I: [BCP App] Dose Rounds<=
/h2>
<p></p>
<p><strong>JIRA Story Link</strong></p>
<div class=3D"table-wrap">
<table data-table-width=3D"1800" data-layout=3D"default" data-local-id=3D"c=
f524cde-b085-4b6e-9784-22777b1925a0" class=3D"confluenceTable">
<colgroup>
<col style=3D"width: 59.0px;">
<col style=3D"width: 701.0px;">
</colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<th class=3D"confluenceTh">
<p>JIRA</p></th>
<td class=3D"confluenceTd">
<p><span class=3D"confluence-jim-macro jira-issue resolved" data-jira-key=
=3D"BMED-10507"> <a href=3D"https://besthealthsolutions.atlassian.net/brows=
e/BMED-10507" class=3D"jira-issue-key"><img class=3D"icon" src=3D"https://b=
esthealthsolutions.atlassian.net/rest/api/2/universal_avatar/view/type/issu=
etype/avatar/10315?size=3Dmedium">BMED-10507</a> - <span class=3D"summary">=
[BCP][App] Dose Rounds</span> <span class=3D"aui-lozenge aui-lozenge-subtle=
 aui-lozenge-success jira-macro-single-issue-export-pdf">Done</span> </span=
></p></td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
</div>
<p><strong>Requirements</strong></p>
<ol start=3D"1">
<li>
<p>The number of rounds and dose times will reflect what the facility has s=
et in Dose Round Config in BESTpack.</p></li>
<li>
<p>When the dose round starts and ends will reflect what the facility has s=
et in the =E2=80=98Start of Round=E2=80=99 and =E2=80=98End of Round=E2=80=
=99 sections in Dose Round Config in BESTpack.</p></li>
<li>
<p>The user will be able to see the previous day, current day, and future d=
ay dose rounds</p></li>
<li>
<p>The colours for dose rounds will reflect what is currently in the web ap=
plication.</p></li>
<li>
<p>The doseround is generated by offline app from date of activation, based=
 on the active medprofile that had been synced.</p></li>
<li>
<p>The structure of the times will reflect what is currently in the web app=
lication. I.e. open and future rounds will have start and finish times in b=
rackets.</p></li>
<li>
<p>When a facility does not have a resident that has a special dose round, =
then there will be no dose rounds displayed beneath =E2=80=98Special Dose R=
ound=E2=80=99</p></li>
<li>
<p>When a facility has a resident that has a special dose round, then that =
dose round will be displayed under =E2=80=98Special Dose Round=E2=80=99.</p=
></li>
<li>
<p>The Special Dose setting &nbsp;for =E2=80=98Start of Round=E2=80=99 and =
=E2=80=98End of Round=E2=80=99 will reflect what the facility has set in Do=
se Round Config in BESTpack.</p></li>
<li>
<p>Display =E2=80=98Out of Dose Round=E2=80=99 button to the right of the =
=E2=80=98Dose Rounds=E2=80=99 heading.</p></li>
<li>
<p>The app will not support Continuous Infusion.</p>
<ol start=3D"1">
<li>
<p>Given the facility has Enable Continuous Infusion ticked in facility set=
tings in BESTpack&nbsp;AND if at least 1 resident in the facility currently=
 has medications prescribed which are marked as 'Continuous Infusion' sched=
ule, then the =E2=80=98Continuous Infusion=E2=80=99 will not appear. &nbsp;=
</p></li>
</ol></li>
<li>
<p><span class=3D"inline-comment-marker" data-ref=3D"1e32977d-8156-4c0f-9f4=
9-7bf35042fd81">When the facility has ticked =E2=80=9CDose Round Extension=
=E2=80=9D in BESTdose Facility Management, then the dose rounds will be ext=
ended as per time set out in settings. </span></p></li>
<li>
<p>The screen will follow the same rules as Dose Rounds in Desktop version =
except for sections that are not part of MVP.</p></li>
<li>
<p>The time remaining will appear as per existing functionality in BESTdose=
</p></li>
</ol>
<h2 id=3D"BCPApp:DoseRounds-II:[BCPApp]MainDoseRoundScreen">II: [BCP App] M=
ain Dose Round Screen</h2>
<p></p>
<p><strong>JIRA Story Link</strong></p>
<div class=3D"table-wrap">
<table data-table-width=3D"1800" data-layout=3D"default" data-local-id=3D"8=
2eb7ac1-076c-4f1b-90a4-4aa965b2e95e" class=3D"confluenceTable">
<colgroup>
<col style=3D"width: 59.0px;">
<col style=3D"width: 701.0px;">
</colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<th class=3D"confluenceTh">
<p>JIRA</p></th>
<td class=3D"confluenceTd">
<p><span class=3D"confluence-jim-macro jira-issue resolved" data-jira-key=
=3D"BMED-9958"> <a href=3D"https://besthealthsolutions.atlassian.net/browse=
/BMED-9958" class=3D"jira-issue-key"><img class=3D"icon" src=3D"https://bes=
thealthsolutions.atlassian.net/rest/api/2/universal_avatar/view/type/issuet=
ype/avatar/10315?size=3Dmedium">BMED-9958</a> - <span class=3D"summary">[BC=
P][App] Main Dose Round Screen</span> <span class=3D"aui-lozenge aui-lozeng=
e-subtle aui-lozenge-success jira-macro-single-issue-export-pdf">Done</span=
> </span></p></td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
</div>
<p><strong>Requirements</strong></p>
<ol start=3D"1">
<li>
<p>When the user has clicked on a time block on the Dose Rounds screen, the=
n the Main Dose Round screen will load.</p></li>
<li>
<p>Underneath the header, display the back bar.</p>
<ol start=3D"1">
<li>
<p>On the left will be the back button.</p></li>
<li>
<p>In the centre will be the title 'Main Dose Round - [Time of Dose Round] =
(Date DD/MM)</p></li>
</ol></li>
<li>
<p>Underneath the back button, on the left side have the label =E2=80=98Sum=
mary=E2=80=99. Appears on the page title.</p></li>
<li>
<p>To the right of the =E2=80=98Summary=E2=80=99 label, include a search ba=
r.</p>
<ol start=3D"1">
<li>
<p>Label 'Residents:'. To be placed to the left of the search bar</p></li>
<li>
<p><span class=3D"inline-comment-marker" data-ref=3D"a9d4db4f-512b-4f23-940=
6-7b063b002535">In search bar, include text: =E2=80=98Search=E2=80=99 and m=
agnifying glass icon. </span></p>
<ol start=3D"1">
<li>
<p>When a user enters in text in the search bar, then the text =E2=80=98Sea=
rch=E2=80=99 will disappear and the text the user has entered will appear.<=
/p></li>
<li>
<p>When a user enters a resident=E2=80=99s name that doesn't exist or is in=
active, then display: =E2=80=9CNo Residents Found!=E2=80=9D below Resident<=
/p></li>
<li>
<p>The magnifying glass icon is not clickable, just for visual cue to searc=
h.</p></li>
</ol></li>
</ol></li>
<li>
<p>To the right of the search bar, include the ability to sort by name and =
room</p>
<ol start=3D"1">
<li>
<p>Label =E2=80=98Sort by:=E2=80=99. To be placed to the left of the radio =
buttons</p></li>
<li>
<p>Label for radio button 1: =E2=80=98Name=E2=80=99</p></li>
<li>
<p>Label for radio button 2: =E2=80=98Room=E2=80=99</p></li>
<li>
<p>When the user presses =E2=80=98Name=E2=80=99 button, then order the pati=
ents by Surname then First name in ascending order.</p></li>
<li>
<p>When the user presses =E2=80=98Room=E2=80=99 button, then</p>
<ol start=3D"1">
<li>
<p>If the rooms are numerically labelled, then order by numerical value in =
ascending order</p></li>
<li>
<p>If the rooms are alphabetically labelled, then order by alphabet in asce=
nding order</p></li>
<li>
<p>If the rooms are alphanumerically labelled, then numbers are sorted befo=
re alphabet (0-9 before A-Z)</p></li>
</ol></li>
</ol></li>
<li>
<p>Display the tabs (Dose Round Filters) that have been set up in Facility =
Config (max of 6 tabs).</p>
<ol start=3D"1">
<li>
<p>Tabs will be in order that they appear in Facility Config.</p></li>
<li>
<p>If there are patients that are in the specific filters, then display the=
 number of patients that correspond to that filter in a red circle to the r=
ight of the filter name with white number.</p></li>
<li>
<p><span class=3D"inline-comment-marker" data-ref=3D"86a9aa0f-0011-4bf2-915=
a-3c6090c9c45e">If there are no patients that are in the specific filter, t=
hen </span></p>
<ol start=3D"1">
<li>
<p><span class=3D"inline-comment-marker" data-ref=3D"86a9aa0f-0011-4bf2-915=
a-3c6090c9c45e">Display a white 0 in a red circle for that filter</span></p=
></li>
<li>
<p>Display: =E2=80=9CNo Residents Found!=E2=80=9D below Resident</p></li>
</ol></li>
<li>
<p>The =E2=80=98All=E2=80=99 filter will display the number of all patients=
 that have meds in that dose round</p></li>
</ol></li>
<li>
<p>Display a table with the following headings:</p>
<ol start=3D"1">
<li>
<p>Resident</p>
<ol start=3D"1">
<li>
<p>Display only residents that have medication to be dispensed in this dose=
 round</p></li>
<li>
<p>Resident photo - display photo linked to resident.<span class=3D"inline-=
comment-marker" data-ref=3D"53f801a7-5058-48df-9a64-01bd3624edeb"> When the=
re is no photo, then display the same icon as per normal BESTdose website. =
</span></p></li>
<li>
<p>To the right of the resident photo, <span class=3D"inline-comment-marker=
" data-ref=3D"e3ea90ac-2ee8-478f-bf94-097a54340773">display resident's name=
: [SURNAME, First name][Preferred Name]</span></p></li>
</ol></li>
<li>
<p>DOB</p>
<ol start=3D"1">
<li>
<p>Format - DD/MM/YYYY</p></li>
</ol></li>
<li>
<p>Section</p></li>
<li>
<p>Room</p></li>
<li>
<p>Notes</p>
<ol start=3D"1">
<li>
<p>For the URNMRN if one is present</p></li>
</ol></li>
</ol></li>
<li>
<p>When the last 30 mins of the dose round extension, then display the time=
 remaining.</p>
<ol start=3D"1">
<li>
<p>Label: 'Time Remaining'. To be placed to the right of the Dose Round Hea=
ding.</p></li>
<li>
<p>Count down begins when there is 30 minutes left in dose round.</p></li>
<li>
<p>When the count down is at 00:00, the dose round is closed</p></li>
</ol></li>
<li>
<p>
<del><span class=3D"inline-comment-marker" data-ref=3D"a0e6a8ea-45e8-495d-9=
fa8-13a616079bc8">Missed Count Indicator </span>- only applies for AIN role=
.</del></p>
<ol start=3D"1">
<li>
<p>
<del>When there is a discrepancy with the dosage and number given, display =
the missed count indicator.</del></p></li>
<li>
<p>
<del>The missed sign indicator will appear on two screens: The Dose Rounds =
and the Main Dose Round.</del></p></li>
</ol></li>
<li>
<p>Display =E2=80=98Similar Name=E2=80=99</p>
<ol start=3D"1">
<li>
<p>Using the SQL Server SOUNDEX() Function to display =E2=80=98Similar Name=
=E2=80=99 badge.</p></li>
<li>
<p>Hesham to provide visual</p></li>
</ol></li>
<li>
<p>If the resident has a URNMRN, then this will be displayed in the notes c=
olumn</p></li>
<li>
<p>When the user has confirmed that the resident has taken their meds, then=
 when they come back to the Main Dose Round screen, that patient will be re=
moved from the list</p></li>
<li>
<p>When the resident=E2=80=99s meds have been administered, they will be re=
moved from the dose round.</p></li>
</ol>
<p>Time Sensitive Meds <a href=3D"https://www.figma.com/design/3mEBxpW3AU6a=
gtPHiikZD5/BESTMED-Modernisation---Revised?node-id=3D5670-14491&amp;t=3DMJh=
cBU9Pj1GGrR9N-4" data-card-appearance=3D"inline" class=3D"external-link" re=
l=3D"nofollow">https://www.figma.com/design/3mEBxpW3AU6agtPHiikZD5/BESTMED-=
Modernisation---Revised?node-id=3D5670-14491&amp;t=3DMJhcBU9Pj1GGrR9N-4</a>=
 :</p>
<ol start=3D"1">
<li>
<p>When the dose round contains time sensitive meds, then</p>
<ol start=3D"1">
<li>
<p>Any resident that has time sensitive meds will be displayed in this sect=
ion AND</p></li>
<li>
<p>Time Sensitive Medication section will be at the top of the page AND</p>=
</li>
<li>
<p>The time sensitive banner will display (blue) AND</p></li>
<li>
<p>The count down timer will display</p></li>
</ol></li>
<li>
<p><span class=3D"inline-comment-marker" data-ref=3D"e13f9ec1-a315-4254-94a=
d-4d25c155ddcb">The countdown time is for 30 minutes AND starts to count do=
wn from 30 minutes when the dose round begins.</span></p></li>
<li>
<p>When the countdown timer is 5 minutes before it expires, then the colour=
 will change to orange</p></li>
<li>
<p>When the countdown timer has finished, then the colour will change to re=
d.</p></li>
</ol>
<h2 id=3D"BCPApp:DoseRounds-III:[BCP][App]DoseRoundResidentInfo-PatientDeta=

ion</h2>

<p><span class=3D"confluence-jim-macro jira-issue resolved" data-jira-key=

<p><strong>Requirements</strong></p>
<ol start=3D"1">
<li>
<p>When the user has clicked on a patient in the<span class=3D"inline-comme=
nt-marker" data-ref=3D"ba779d6c-f463-4ff0-8552-006816e17668"> Main Dose Rou=
nd, Special Dose Round OR Out of Dose Round screen</span>, then the Dose Ro=
und Resident info screen will load</p></li>
<li>
<p>Underneath the header, display the back bar.</p>
<ol start=3D"1">
<li>
<p>On the left will be the back button.</p></li>
<li>
<p>When it is the Main Dose Round, then in the center will be the title =E2=
=80=98Main Dose Round - [Time of Dose Round] (Date DD/MM)=E2=80=99</p></li>
<li>
<p>When it is the Special Dose Round, then in the center will be the title =
=E2=80=98Special Dose Round - [Time of Dose Round] (Date DD/MM)=E2=80=99</p=
></li>
<li>
<p>When it is the Out Dose Round, then in the center will be the title =E2=
=80=98Out Dose Round (Date DD/MM)=E2=80=99</p></li>
</ol></li>
<li>
<p><span class=3D"inline-comment-marker" data-ref=3D"03e38888-2789-4c6f-a2c=
0-79d1d41428e4">Display the Resident profile on the left side of the screen=
.</span></p>
<ol start=3D"1">
<li>
<p>Resident photo</p></li>
<li>
<p>Surname and First name displayed below photo</p></li>
<li>
<p>Date of Photo: [DD/MM/YY]</p></li>
<li>
<p>MIN</p>
<ol start=3D"1">
<li>
<p>When there is a value in URN/MRN/MIN</p></li>
</ol></li>
<li>
<p>Resident</p></li>
<li>
<p>DOB: DD/MM/YYYY</p></li>
<li>
<p>Prescriber</p></li>
<li>
<p>Prescriber No.</p></li>
<li>
<p>Room No.</p></li>
<li>
<p>Section</p></li>
<li>
<p>Pharmacy</p></li>
<li>
<p><span class=3D"inline-comment-marker" data-ref=3D"c4d927dc-95bb-4f52-9cd=
d-3be33c227532">Chart Cycle - display as Red/Orange/Green as per existing f=
unctionality</span></p></li>
<li>
<p><span class=3D"inline-comment-marker" data-ref=3D"c4d927dc-95bb-4f52-9cd=
d-3be33c227532">Chart Last Updated - display as Red/Orange/Green as per exi=
sting functionality</span></p></li>
<li>
<p>No PRAT available</p>
<ol start=3D"1">
<li>
<p>As per existing logic <a href=3D"https://besthealthsolutions.atlassian.n=
et/wiki/spaces/DO/pages/1898774601/Serco+Add+No+PRAT+available+indication+i=
n+Resident+Demographics+section+across+BESTdose+i.e.+Dose+Rounds+etc#Serco:=
Add&amp;" data-linked-resource-id=3D"1898774601" data-linked-resource-versi=
on=3D"2" data-linked-resource-type=3D"page">Serco: Add 'No PRAT available' =
indication in Resident Demographics section across BESTdose (i.e. Dose Roun=
ds, etc)</a></p></li>
<li>
<p>Will appear in</p>
<ol start=3D"1">
<li>
<p>Medication Rounds</p></li>
<li>
<p>OBS</p></li>
</ol></li>
</ol></li>
</ol></li>
<li>
<p>To the right of the Resident Profile, display the following:</p>
<ol start=3D"1">
<li>
<p>Complex Med Alert</p>
<ol start=3D"1">
<li>
<p>Heading is in red</p></li>
<li>
<p>Data is pulled from BESTMED</p></li>
<li>
<p>Given there is data in BESTMED, then this data will be displayed</p></li=
>
<li>
<p><span class=3D"inline-comment-marker" data-ref=3D"57e43690-ed87-4366-a71=
7-6fb35bf311ca">Given there is no data in BESTMED then the section will not=
 be displayed. </span></p></li>
</ol></li>
<li>
<p>Allergies and Adverse Drug Reactions:</p>
<ol start=3D"1">
<li>
<p>Heading is in red</p></li>
<li>
<p>Data is pulled from BESTMED</p></li>
<li>
<p><span class=3D"inline-comment-marker" data-ref=3D"b26332bc-6c52-4720-bdf=
f-007490b6db27">When there is data in BESTMED, then this data will be displ=
ayed </span></p></li>
<li>
<p>When there is no data in BESTMED, there no data will be displayed</p></l=
i>
<li>
<p>When the =E2=80=98Nil Known=E2=80=99 is selected in BESTdoctor, then dis=
play =E2=80=9CNil Known=E2=80=9D</p></li>
</ol></li>
<li>
<p>Considerations</p>
<ol start=3D"1">
<li>
<p>Data is pulled from BESTMED</p></li>
<li>
<p>Given there is data in BESTMED, then this data will be displayed.</p></l=
i>
<li>
<p>Given there is no data in BESTMED, then only the title will be displayed=
.</p></li>
</ol></li>
<li>
<p>Diagnosis</p>
<ol start=3D"1">
<li>
<p>Data is pulled from BESTMED</p></li>
<li>
<p>Given there is data in BESTMED, then this data will be displayed.</p></l=
i>
<li>
<p>Given there is no data in BESTMED, then only the title will be displayed=
.</p></li>
</ol></li>
<li>
<p>Important MedRound Notes</p>
<ol start=3D"1">
<li>
<p>Data is pulled from BESTMED</p></li>
<li>
<p>Given there is data in BESTMED, then this data will be displayed.</p></l=
i>
<li>
<p>Given there is no data in BESTMED, then only the title will be displayed=
.</p></li>
<li>
<p>The edit button will not be displayed</p></li>
</ol></li>
</ol></li>
<li>

<p>OBS</p></li>

<p>Emergency Stock</p></li>
<li>
<p>Medication Chart</p></li>
</ol></li>
<li>
<p>When the user loads the screen, the =E2=80=98Dose Round=E2=80=99 tab is =
the default tab.</p></li>
<li>
<p>Do not show =E2=80=9CMedication Chart is expired=E2=80=9D pop-up for the=
 resident that has expired chart. Both BESTdose and BESTdoctor are locked d=
own during offline, therefore asking prescriber to review medchart is not n=
ecessary</p></li>

</p></li>

utton, then the =E2=80=98Confirm Incident Report for [SURNAME, Firstname] m=
odal appears.</del></p></li>

=9CAdmin=E2=80=9D check box, then display a pop up</p>

</ol></li>

ccess=E2=80=99, =E2=80=98Save Success=E2=80=99, or =E2=80=98Successfully Sa=
ved=E2=80=99</p></li>

<p><strong>INR</strong></p>
<ol start=3D"1">
<li>

<del>hen 'Force INR recording prior to Variable administration=E2=80=99 is =

ication.</del></p></li>

<li>

<li>
<p>When =E2=80=98Force INR recording prior to Variable administration=E2=80=
=99 is ticked in BESTpack AND the resident has Variable medication, show =
=E2=80=9CRecord INR=E2=80=9D button and text box instead of =E2=80=98INR Re=
ading Required=E2=80=99 pop up for administration. Example:</p><span class=

<p>If the user enters a different dosage amount to what is displayed in =E2=
=80=98Prescribed=E2=80=99, when they try and administer the medication, the=
n a warning will be displayed within the modal.</p></li>
</ol>
<p><strong>ALERTS</strong></p>
<ol start=3D"1">
<li>
<p>Given the DR ticked =E2=80=98Yes=E2=80=99 on =E2=80=98Is this medication=
 being used as a Chemical Restraint=E2=80=99 in the Psychotropic Assessment=
, then the =E2=80=98Restrictive Practice - Chemical Restraint=E2=80=99 tag&=
nbsp;will appear against that medication.</p></li>
<li>
<p>Given the Prescriber ticked =E2=80=98Unusual Dose' in the Administration=
 Options section in BESTdoctor, then the 'Unusual Dose=E2=80=99 tag will ap=
pear against that med in the Dosage column.</p></li>
<li>
<p>Given the Prescriber ticked =E2=80=98Self Administered' in the Administr=
ation Options section in BESTdoctor, when then the page lands, the =E2=80=
=98Reason=E2=80=99 column is greyed out and =E2=80=98Self Administered=E2=
=80=99 selected.&nbsp;</p></li>
<li>
<p>Given the Prescriber ticked =E2=80=98Do Not Crush' in the Administration=
 Options section in BESTdoctor, when then the page lands, the =E2=80=98Do N=
ot Crush=E2=80=99 icon will appear in ROA column. &nbsp;&nbsp;</p></li>
<li>
<p>Borders and Badges =E2=80=93 display the appropriate border and badge wh=
en the dose medicine is:</p>
<ol start=3D"1">
<li>
<p>Dark Purple =3D Cytotoxic medication - #3B0944</p></li>
<li>
<p>Light Purple =3D Hazardous medication (previously Cytostatic medication)=
 - #CBC9FF</p></li>
<li>
<p>Pink =3D Nutritional - #FFABE5</p></li>
<li>
<p>Yellow =3D Warfarin - #FAEE5A</p></li>
<li>
<p>Brown =3D Insulin - #B2704E</p></li>
<li>
<p>Green =3D s8 medication - #067242</p></li>
<li>
<p>Black =3D Short course medication - #00000</p></li>
<li>
<p>Maroon=3D S4D medication - #800000</p></li>
</ol></li>
</ol>
<p><strong>PATCH</strong></p>
<ol start=3D"1">
<li>
<p>When =E2=80=98Check Patch=E2=80=99 is ticked in BESTpack AND times have =
been entered in =E2=80=98Select Check Patch Times=E2=80=99 AND the patch wa=
s applied 24 hours ago, THEN the =E2=80=98Check Patch=E2=80=99 option will =
be listed in the dose round at the time closest to =E2=80=98Select Check Pa=
tch Times=E2=80=99 24 hours after patch applied.</p></li>
<li>
<p>When =E2=80=98Remove Patch=E2=80=99 is ticked in BESTpack AND the value =
entered in =E2=80=98Patch Duration=E2=80=99 in BESTdoctor has passed, then =
the =E2=80=98Remove Patch=E2=80=99 option will be listed in the dose round =
before the line for administering the patch.</p></li>
<li>
<p>When =E2=80=98Patch Site=E2=80=99 is ticked in BESTpack AND the resident=
 has a patch prescribed, then</p>
<ol start=3D"1">
<li>
<p>The patch site icon will appear, AND</p></li>
<li>
<p>The user will be required to select patch site when administering patch.=
</p></li>
</ol></li>
<li>
<p><span class=3D"inline-comment-marker" data-ref=3D"a110d0cc-03ef-4edb-ac0=
5-c3af072fa3a6">When the schedule for the patch has been updated via BESTdo=
se, then it will NOT impact the schedule for the offline app. I.e. the offl=
ine app will follow the dosage from BESTdoctor</span></p></li>
<li>
<p>There will be no ability to reapply a patch in the offline app</p>
<ol start=3D"1">
<li>
<p>Given the =E2=80=9CCheck Patch=E2=80=9D is displayed in the dose rounds,=
 when the user clicks on the Reason drop down, then the =E2=80=9CRe-apply P=
atch=E2=80=9D option will not be visible.</p></li>
</ol></li>
<li>
<p>The =E2=80=9CView Patch Site History=E2=80=9D button will not be visible=
 in the offline app</p></li>
<li>
<p>Preferred patch is not supported in phase 1.</p>
<ol start=3D"1">
<li>
<p>Example: readonly Comment in patch site pop-up will not be shown as it=
=E2=80=99s related to preferred patch.</p></li>
</ol></li>
<li>
<p>In Phase 1, as no history is synced, app will recognize the existing pat=
ch as a new patch for the first day activation</p></li>
<li>
<p>No need to show =E2=80=9CRestrictive Practice=E2=80=9D flag in the Check=
 Patch</p></li>
</ol>
<p>&nbsp;<strong>INSULIN - BGL</strong></p>
<ol start=3D"1">
<li>
<p>When =E2=80=98Force BGL recording prior to Insulin administration=E2=80=
=99 is ticked in BESTpack AND the resident has Insulin prescribed, then</p>
<ol start=3D"1">
<li>
<p>The BGL Reading Required icon will be displayed next to the medication n=
ame, AND</p></li>
<li>
<p>=E2=80=98BGL Required prior to administration=E2=80=99 will be displayed=
 in red at top of that medication section, AND</p></li>
<li>
<p>The BGL section will be displayed (field to enter value and =E2=80=98Rec=
ord BGL=E2=80=99) , AND</p>
<ol start=3D"1">
<li>
<p>BGL History will not be visible</p></li>
</ol></li>
<li>
<p>The user will need to enter the BGL prior to administering Insulin.</p><=
/li>
</ol></li>
<li>
<p>When the user records the BGL level on the Dose Round screen, then</p>
<ol start=3D"1">
<li>
<p>Under Reason column it displays =E2=80=98Not Required=E2=80=99 AND</p></=
li>
<li>
<p>The value entered for BGL and time is displayed =E2=80=93 =E2=80=98BGL [=
Value N.NNN] recorded at [DD/MM] [HHMM]=E2=80=99 AND</p></li>
<li>
<p>The colour of the =E2=80=98Record BGL=E2=80=99 button is muted AND</p></=
li>
<li>
<p>The Admin tickbox is removed and replaced with =E2=80=98-=E2=80=98.</p><=
/li>
</ol></li>
<li>
<p>When =E2=80=98Force BGL recording prior to Insulin administration=E2=80=
=99 is ticked in BESTpack&nbsp; AND the user has not entered the BGL level =
on the Dose Round screen, when they attempt to administer medication, then =
the =E2=80=98BGL Reading Required=E2=80=99 modal pops up.</p></li>
<li>
<p>When the user enters a value in the =E2=80=98BGL Reading Required=E2=80=
=99 modal, then the =E2=80=98Insulin Sliding Scale Directions=E2=80=99 moda=
l is displayed.</p></li>
<li>
<p>When the =E2=80=98Insulin Sliding Scale Directions=E2=80=99 modal is dis=
played:</p>
<ol start=3D"1">
<li>
<p>If the user enters a value in =E2=80=98Administered dosage=E2=80=99 that=
 is the same as the BESTMED calculated value, then the user can proceed to =
the next step</p></li>
<li>
<p>If the user enters a value in =E2=80=98Administered dosage=E2=80=99 that=
 is different to the BESTMED calculated value, then the modal expands with =
the =E2=80=98Reason For Change:=E2=80=99 section AND the user has to enter =
data in the text box before they can proceed.</p></li>
</ol></li>
<li>
<p>
<del>When the user clicks on =E2=80=98View BGL History=E2=80=99, then the B=
GL table modal will display with the following headings:</del></p>
<ol start=3D"1">
<li>
<p>
<del>Date and Time [DD/MM/YYY] [HHMM]</del></p></li>
<li>
<p>
<del>Observation (mmol/L) [V.VVV]</del></p></li>
<li>
<p>
<del>Prescriber Range Below Limit</del></p></li>
<li>
<p>
<del>Prescriber Range Above Limit</del></p></li>
</ol></li>
<li>
<p>When then prescriber has entered data into the sliding scale table, then=
 the =E2=80=98BGL Required=E2=80=99 icon is displayed AND the user will nee=
d to enter the BGL prior to administering the medication.</p></li>
</ol>
<p>&nbsp;<strong><span class=3D"inline-comment-marker" data-ref=3D"d95854a4=
-89b1-46f4-b953-e2731a20ef05">DUAL SIGN</span></strong></p>
<ol start=3D"1">
<li>
<p>When =E2=80=98Dual signing required for Insulin=E2=80=99 is ticked in BE=
STpack AND the resident has Insulin prescribed, then</p>
<ol start=3D"1">
<li>
<p>Then the dual sign icon will appear next to the medication name AND</p><=
/li>
<li>
<p>When the drug is selected to be administered, the dual sign modal will a=
ppear.&nbsp;</p></li>
</ol></li>
<li>
<p>When =E2=80=98Dual signing required for S4D administration=E2=80=99 is t=
icked in BESTpack AND the resident has S4D meds prescribed, then</p>
<ol start=3D"1">
<li>
<p>Then the dual sign icon will appear next to the medication name AND</p><=
/li>
<li>
<p>When the drug is selected to be administered, the dual sign modal will a=
ppear.&nbsp;</p></li>
</ol></li>
<li>
<p>When =E2=80=98Dual signing required for S8 administration=E2=80=99 is ti=
cked in BESTpack AND the resident has S8 meds prescribed, then</p>
<ol start=3D"1">
<li>
<p>Then the dual sign icon will appear next to the medication name AND</p><=
/li>
<li>
<p>When the drug is selected to be administered, the dual sign modal will a=
ppear.&nbsp;</p></li>
</ol></li>
<li>
<p>When =E2=80=98Dual signing required for S8 Patch Removal=E2=80=99 is tic=
ked in BESTpack AND the resident has S8 meds prescribed, then</p>
<ol start=3D"1">
<li>
<p>Then the dual sign icon will appear next to the medication name AND</p><=
/li>
<li>
<p>When the drug is selected to be administered, the dual sign modal will a=
ppear.&nbsp;</p></li>
</ol></li>
<li>
<p>When =E2=80=98Dual signing required for injection administration=E2=80=
=99 is ticked in BESTpack AND the resident has one of the following ROA =E2=
=80=93 Intra-articular, Intramuscular, Intravenous, Intravesical, Subcutane=
ous, Subcutaneous Infusion - prescribed, then</p>
<ol start=3D"1">
<li>
<p>Then the dual sign icon will appear next to the medication name AND</p><=
/li>
<li>
<p>When the drug is selected to be administered, the dual sign modal will a=
ppear.&nbsp;</p></li>
</ol></li>
<li>
<p>When =E2=80=98Dual signing required for Variable administration=E2=80=99=
 is ticked in BESTpack AND the resident has variable medication prescribed,=
 then</p>
<ol start=3D"1">
<li>
<p>Then the dual sign icon will appear next to the medication name AND</p><=
/li>
<li>
<p>When the drug is selected to be administered, the dual sign modal will a=
ppear.&nbsp;</p></li>
</ol></li>
<li>
<p>When =E2=80=98Dual signing required for Hazardous Cytotoxic administrati=
on=E2=80=99 is ticked in BESTpack AND the resident has Hazardous Cytotoxic =
prescribed, then</p>
<ol start=3D"1">
<li>
<p>Then the dual sign icon will appear next to the medication name AND</p><=
/li>
<li>
<p>When the drug is selected to be administered, the dual sign modal will a=
ppear.&nbsp;</p></li>
</ol></li>
<li>
<p>When =E2=80=98Dual signing required for Not-Hazardous Cytotoxic administ=
ration=E2=80=99 is ticked in BESTpack AND the resident has Not-Hazardous Cy=
totoxic prescribed, then</p>
<ol start=3D"1">
<li>
<p>Then the dual sign icon will appear next to the medication name AND</p><=
/li>
<li>
<p>When the drug is selected to be administered, the dual sign modal will a=
ppear.&nbsp;</p></li>
</ol></li>
<li>
<p>Agency users will not be able to dual sign</p>
<ol start=3D"1">
<li>
<p>Same functionality will exist for when user who is not authorised to dua=
l sign enters PIN</p></li>
</ol></li>
<li>
<p>Users who have permission to dual sign but do not have login access to t=
he app will be able to dual sign</p></li>
</ol>
<p><strong>SHORT COURSE</strong></p>
<ol start=3D"1">
<li>
<p>When the medication status is inactive in the backend, then the medicati=
on will not appear in the dose rounds.</p></li>
<li>
<p>When the medication status is active in the backend, then the medication=
 will appear in the specified dose rounds.</p></li>
</ol>
<p><strong>TIME SENSITIVE MEDS</strong></p>
<ol start=3D"1">
<li>
<p>When the dose round contains time sensitive meds, then</p>
<ol start=3D"1">
<li>
<p>The time sensitive banner will be displayed AND</p></li>
<li>
<p>The countdown timer will display</p></li>
</ol></li>
<li>
<p>The countdown time is for 30 minutes AND starts to count down from 30 mi=
nutes when the dose round begins.</p></li>
<li>
<p>When there is 5 minutes left until countdown timer expires, then the col=
our will change to orange</p></li>
<li>
<p>When the countdown timer has finished, then</p>
<ol start=3D"1">
<li>
<p>The colour will change to red AND</p></li>
<li>
<p>The user can still administer the medication</p></li>
</ol></li>
</ol>

<h2 id=3D"BCPApp:DoseRounds-V:[BCPApp]AINRecordAdministration">
<del>V: [BCP App] AIN Record Administration</del></h2>
<p></p>
<p><strong>JIRA Story Link</strong></p>
<div class=3D"table-wrap">
<table data-table-width=3D"1800" data-layout=3D"default" data-local-id=3D"d=

<p>JIRA</p></th>
<td class=3D"confluenceTd">
<p><span class=3D"confluence-jim-macro jira-issue resolved" data-jira-key=
=3D"BMED-10171"> <a href=3D"https://besthealthsolutions.atlassian.net/brows=
e/BMED-10171" class=3D"jira-issue-key"><img class=3D"icon" src=3D"https://b=

<p>For MVP, AIN will not be able to access the app</p>
<p><strong>Requirements</strong></p>
<p>These requirements are for when an AIN signs in to BESTdose as they have=
 to count PACKED meds.</p>
<p>PACKED section:</p>
<ol start=3D"1">
<li>
<p>When the AIN is on the Dose Round Tab, then the =E2=80=98Reason=E2=80=99=
 drop down will be disabled AND the Admin tick box will be replaced with th=
e =E2=80=98RN=E2=80=99 tick box.</p></li>
<li>
<p>When the =E2=80=98RN=E2=80=99 tick box is clicked, then the =E2=80=98Sec=
ondary Authentication Required=E2=80=99 modal will appear</p></li>
<li>
<p>Underneath the Packed section, display =E2=80=98Number Given=E2=80=99 an=
d =E2=80=98Reason=E2=80=99 box</p></li>
<li>
<p>The user can enter numbers in =E2=80=98Number Given=E2=80=99 box</p>
<ul>
<li>
<p>When the user presses the box, then the keypad will appear at the bottom=
 of the screen</p></li>
</ul></li>
<li>
<p>The =E2=80=98Reason=E2=80=99 box is a drop down, with the following opti=
ons:</p>
<ul>
<li>
<p>Absent</p></li>
<li>
<p>Ceased</p></li>
<li>
<p>Fasting</p></li>
<li>
<p>Hospital</p></li>
<li>
<p>No Stock</p></li>
<li>
<p>Omitted</p></li>
<li>
<p>Refused</p></li>
<li>
<p>Self Administered</p></li>
<li>
<p>Social Leave</p></li>
<li>
<p>Withheld</p></li>
</ul></li>
<li>
<p>Given the number entered in the =E2=80=98Number Given=E2=80=99 box is di=
fferent to the dosage amount, when the user clicks on confirm, then the con=
firmation modal appears AND the warning comment in the bottom of the modal =
appears</p></li>
</ol>
<p></p>
<p>NON PACKED section:</p>
<ol start=3D"1">
<li>
<p>Functionality the same as RN.</p></li>
</ol>
<p></p>
<p>Variable Dose Medication section:</p>
<p>AINs are unable to administer variable medication</p>
<ol start=3D"1">
<li>
<p>When the AIN lands on the dose round tab screen AND the resident has var=
iable medication, then the following fields will be disabled:</p>
<ol start=3D"1">
<li>
<p>Prescribed box</p></li>
<li>
<p>Given box</p></li>
<li>
<p>Reason box</p></li>
<li>
<p>Admin box</p></li>
</ol></li>
</ol>
<p></p>
<h2 id=3D"BCPApp:DoseRounds-VI:[BCPApp]OutofDoseRoundscreen">VI: [BCP App] =
Out of Dose Round screen</h2>
<p><strong>JIRA Story Link</strong></p>
<div class=3D"table-wrap">
<table data-table-width=3D"1800" data-layout=3D"default" data-local-id=3D"3=
a45de3b-3077-480e-a1d0-a14c1e56dc4d" class=3D"confluenceTable">
<colgroup>
<col style=3D"width: 59.0px;">
<col style=3D"width: 701.0px;">
</colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<th data-highlight-colour=3D"var(--ds-background-accent-gray-subtlest,#f4f5=
f7)" class=3D"confluenceTh">
<p>JIRA</p></th>
<td class=3D"confluenceTd">
<p>&nbsp; <span class=3D"confluence-jim-macro jira-issue resolved" data-jir=
a-key=3D"BMED-10426"> <a href=3D"https://besthealthsolutions.atlassian.net/=
browse/BMED-10426" class=3D"jira-issue-key"><img class=3D"icon" src=3D"http=
s://besthealthsolutions.atlassian.net/rest/api/2/universal_avatar/view/type=
/issuetype/avatar/10315?size=3Dmedium">BMED-10426</a> - <span class=3D"summ=
ary">[BCP][App] Out of Dose Round Screen</span> <span class=3D"aui-lozenge =
aui-lozenge-subtle aui-lozenge-success jira-macro-single-issue-export-pdf">=
Done</span> </span></p></td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
</div>
<p><strong>Requirements</strong></p>
<ol start=3D"1">
<li>
<p>When the Out of Dose Round page loads, it will have the following:</p>
<ol start=3D"1">
<li>
<p>Heading: Out of Dose Round</p></li>
<li>
<p>Display the date section, accept to select date from date selector</p></=
li>
<li>
<p>Resident section: same as main dose round screen</p></li>
<li>
<p>Table with following columns: Resident, DOB, Section, Room, Note.</p></l=
i>
</ol></li>
<li>
<p>The tabs that are displayed will be the same as what is displayed in Mai=
n Dose Round.</p></li>
<li>
<p>When the user clicks on a resident, then they will see the dose round ti=
mes where the medication has not been administered.</p></li>
<li>
<p>When the resident has no more dose rounds available, then the following =
message will be displayed at the top: =E2=80=98No Regular / Short Course me=
dication available=E2=80=99</p></li>
<li>
<p>When the user clicks on an active dose round, then the functionality wil=
l be the same as the Main Dose Round screen. &nbsp;</p></li>
<li>
<p>When the user clicks on a future dose round (today), then the functional=
ity will be the same as the Main Dose Round screen. &nbsp;</p></li>
<li>
<p>When the user clicks on a closed dose round, can not record the admin as=
 in the main dose round.</p></li>
<li>
<p>When the user selects future dates, and click on any doseround, the medi=
cations are displayed as in web UI, admin checkbox is grey out and there is=
 no more button to admin</p></li>
<li>
<p>&nbsp;When the user administers the medication, then that dose round tim=
e is removed.</p></li>
<li>
<p>Given the user has clicked on open dose round or future dose round (toda=
y), when administering the medication, then it will follow the same process=
 as the web app.</p></li>
<li>
<p>The labels and warnings linked to the medication will be the same as the=
 web app.</p></li>
<li>
<p>The structure of the table that lists medication will be the same as the=
 Main Dose Round screen. (The order column will not be present).</p></li>
<li>
<p>Given the user administers the PRN/NIM/Emergency as the same as Main dos=
e round.</p>
<ol start=3D"1">
<li>
<p>For AIN, should logout and login with RN/EN to administer</p></li>
</ol></li>
<li>
<p>After ending Offline mode</p>
<ol start=3D"1">
<li>
<p>The record on Dose round tab should be updated to Offline_Dosemed table<=
/p></li>
<li>
<p>The record on PRN tab should be updated to Offline_PRNMedSign table</p><=
/li>
<li>
<p>The record on NIM tab should be updated to Offline_NIMSign table</p></li=
>
<li>
<p>The record on Emergency Stock should be updated to Offline_EmergencyMedS=
ign table</p></li>
</ol></li>
</ol>
<h2 id=3D"BCPApp:DoseRounds-VII:[BCPApp]SpecialDoseRoundscreen">VII: [BCP A=

<p><strong>Requirements</strong></p>
<ol start=3D"1">
<li>
<p>When the prescriber has added Special Dose Time for medication in BESTdo=
ctor, then it will appear in the created Special Dose Round.</p></li>
<li>
<p>When the user clicks on a Special Dose Round, then - Special Dose Round =
- [TIME] [(Date)] will be displayed in the back button section.[[</p></li>
<li>
<p>The rest of the functionality will be the same as main dose round.&nbsp;=
</p></li>

<p><strong>Requirements:</strong></p>
<ol start=3D"1">
<li>
<p>When the user clicks on PRN tab, then the PRN screen appears AND [(PRN)]=
 will be displayed in the back button section after the date.</p></li>
<li>
<p>If the resident has no PRN medication, then it will display the followin=
g message =E2=80=9CNo PRN medication available' at the top of that section<=
/p></li>
<li>
<p>If the resident has PRN medication, then it will display the medication =
in the following order:</p>
<ol start=3D"1">
<li>
<p><span class=3D"inline-comment-marker" data-ref=3D"2399e7e2-b8d6-41cf-bf9=
b-5e2d5dc5c331">Packed meds to be display at top and then Non Packed</span>=
 (Regular Medication, <span class=3D"inline-comment-marker" data-ref=3D"13b=
337e6-ba59-4856-8823-eaaa35c0e445">Variable Dose Medications</span>, Insuli=
n) below.</p></li>
<li>
<p>When the resident does not have Packed meds, then Non Packed will be at =
the top</p></li>
</ol></li>
<li>
<p>Display table with following headings:</p>
<ol start=3D"1">
<li>
<p>Medication</p>
<ol start=3D"1">
<li>
<p>Have an image of the medication on the left followed by the medication n=
ame</p></li>
<li>
<p>Below medication name display label =E2=80=98For:=E2=80=99. Data is pull=
ed from =E2=80=98Indication*=E2=80=99 in BESTdose.</p></li>
<li>
<p>If medication is Paracetamol, then hide =E2=80=98Check 24hr Usage=E2=80=
=99 button.</p></li>
</ol></li>
<li>
<p>ROA</p>
<ol start=3D"1">
<li>
<p>Data is pulled from =E2=80=98Route*=E2=80=99 in BESTdose.</p></li>
</ol></li>
<li>
<p>Direction</p>
<ol start=3D"1">
<li>
<p>Data is pulled from =E2=80=98Directions*=E2=80=99 in BESTdose</p></li>
<li>
<p>Frequency is pulled from =E2=80=98PRN Frequency &amp; Dose Times=E2=80=
=99 in BESTdose</p></li>
</ol></li>
<li>
<p>Qty</p>
<ol start=3D"1">
<li>
<p>Numerical value</p></li>
<li>
<p>Below QTY will be the dosing unit. Dosing unit is pulled from =E2=80=98D=
osing Units*=E2=80=99 in BESTdose.</p></li>
</ol></li>
<li>
<p>Admin</p>
<ol start=3D"1">
<li>
<p>Check box</p></li>
</ol></li>
</ol></li>
<li>
<p>
<del>Given the AIN has signed in:</del></p>
<ol start=3D"1">
<li>
<p>
<del>When the AIN enters a value in Qty and ticks Admin, then the PRN Medic=
ation Dosing modal appears (RN or EN pin to confirm)</del></p></li>
<li>
<p>
<del>When the RN/EN enters correct pin in PRN Medication Dosing modal and p=
resses =E2=80=98Verify=E2=80=99, then when the modal closes AND the admin b=
ox is unticked</del></p></li>
<li>
<p>
<del>When the AIN re-ticks the admin box, then the confirmation modal appea=
rs.</del></p></li>
</ol></li>
<li>
<p>When the user has entered a correct value in QTY, ticked Admin box and p=
ressed confirm, then the confirmation modal appears.</p></li>
<li>
<p>Borders and Badges =E2=80=93 display the appropriate border and badge wh=
en the dose medicine is:</p>
<ol start=3D"1">
<li>
<p>Dark Purple =3D Cytotoxic medication - #3B0944</p></li>
<li>
<p>Light Purple =3D Hazardous medication (previously Cytostatic medication)=
 - #CBC9FF</p></li>
<li>
<p>Pink =3D Nutritional - #FFABE5</p></li>
<li>
<p><span class=3D"inline-comment-marker" data-ref=3D"1334d259-ea66-438d-99b=
7-e42fed1c6068">Yellow =3D Warfarin - #FAEE5A</span></p></li>
<li>
<p>Brown =3D Insulin - #B2704E</p></li>
<li>
<p>Green =3D s8 medication - #067242</p></li>
<li>
<p>Black =3D Short course medication - #00000</p></li>
<li>
<p>Maroon=3D S4D medication - #800000</p></li>
</ol></li>
<li>
<p>When =E2=80=98Force BGL recording prior to Insulin administration=E2=80=
=99 is ticked in BESTpack AND the resident has Insulin prescribed in PRN, t=
hen</p>
<ol start=3D"1">
<li>

ame, AND</p></li>
<li>
<p>=E2=80=98BGL Required prior to administration=E2=80=99 will be displayed=
 in red at top of that medication section, AND</p></li>
<li>
<p>The BGL section will be displayed (field to enter value, =E2=80=98Record=
 BGL=E2=80=99 and<span class=3D"inline-comment-marker" data-ref=3D"f9668ad7=
-9f7c-4a28-9778-d18aa6619fdb"> =E2=80=98View BGL History=E2=80=99</span>, A=
ND</p></li>
<li>
<p>The user will need to enter the BGL prior to administering Insulin.</p><=
/li>
</ol></li>
<li>

<ol start=3D"1">
<li>

li>

Value N.NNN] recorded at [DD/MM] [HHMM]=E2=80=99 AND</p></li>

/li>
</ol></li>
<li>

en they attempt to administer medication, then the =E2=80=98BGL Reading Req=
uired=E2=80=99 modal pops up.</p></li>
<li>
<p>When the user enters a value in the =E2=80=98BGL Reading Required=E2=80=
=99 modal, then the =E2=80=98Insulin Sliding Scale Directions=E2=80=99 moda=
l is displayed.</p></li>

 modal is displayed:</span></p>

 is the same as the BESTMED calculated value, then the user can proceed to =

<li>
<p>If the user enters a value in =E2=80=98Administered dosage=E2=80=99 that=
 is different to the BESTMED calculated value, then the modal expands with =

data in the text box before they can proceed.</p></li>

<li>

ot Crush=E2=80=99 icon will appear in ROA column. &nbsp;</p></li>

<del>IX: [BCP App] OBS screen</del></h2>

<p>JIRA</p></th>
<td class=3D"confluenceTd">
<p>&nbsp; <span class=3D"confluence-jim-macro jira-issue resolved" data-jir=

<p>Not doing as part of MVP. Could be part of future release.</p>
<p><strong>Requirements</strong></p>
<ol start=3D"1">
<li>
<p>When the user selects Emergency Stock tab, then the Emergency Stock scre=
en appears AND [(Emgcy Stock)] will be displayed in the back button section=
 after the date.</p></li>
<li>
<p>If the facility has no Emergency Stock listed in BESTpack, then the Medi=
cation headings will have no medications listed</p></li>
<li>
<p>If the facility has Emergency Stock listed in BESTpack, then it will be =
listed on this screen</p></li>
<li>
<p>When there is a medication image available, display this in the space pr=
ovided</p></li>
<li>
<p>When there is no medication image available, display the default image (=
name: camera)</p></li>
<li>
<p>Display medication image, medication name, ROA, Qty, Admin</p></li>
<li>
<p>If medication is Paracetamol, then hide =E2=80=98Check 24hr Usage=E2=80=
=99 button.</p></li>
<li>
<p>When =E2=80=98Force BGL recording prior to Insulin administration=E2=80=
=99 is ticked in BESTpack AND the facility has Insulin listed in Emergency =
Stock then,</p>
<ol start=3D"1">
<li>
<p>The =E2=80=98View BGL History=E2=80=99 section is displayed</p></li>
<li>
<p>The =E2=80=98BGL Reading Required=E2=80=99 icon is displayed,</p></li>
<li>
<p>When the user administers the medication, then the =E2=80=98BGL Reading =
Required=E2=80=99 modal will display</p></li>
</ol></li>
<li>
<p>When the 'Check Pulse for Digoxin=E2=80=99 ticked in BESTpack AND the fa=
cility has Digoxin listed in Emergency Stock then,</p>
<ol start=3D"1">
<li>
<p>The heartbeat icon is displayed,</p></li>
<li>
<p>The =E2=80=98View Pulse History' section is displayed</p></li>
<li>
<p>When the user administers the medication, then the =E2=80=98Pulse Readin=
g Required=E2=80=99 modal will display</p></li>
</ol></li>
<li>
<p>If the =E2=80=98Insulin Site Required' icon is displayed, when the user =
administers the medication, then the =E2=80=98Insulin Injection Site Requir=
ed=E2=80=99 modal will appear</p></li>
<li>
<p>If the =E2=80=98Dual Signing=E2=80=99 icon is displayed, when the user a=
dministers the medication, then the =E2=80=98Secondary Authentication Requi=
red' modal will appear</p></li>
<li>
<p>Borders and Badges =E2=80=93 display the appropriate border and badge wh=
en the dose medicine is:</p>
<ol start=3D"1">
<li>
<p>Dark Purple =3D Cytotoxic medication - #3B0944</p></li>
<li>
<p>Light Purple =3D Hazardous medication (previously Cytostatic medication)=
 - #CBC9FF</p></li>
<li>
<p>Pink =3D Nutritional - #FFABE5</p></li>
<li>
<p>Yellow =3D Warfarin - #FAEE5A</p></li>
<li>
<p>Brown =3D Insulin - #B2704E</p></li>
<li>
<p>Green =3D s8 medication - #067242</p></li>
<li>
<p>Black =3D Short course medication - #00000</p></li>
<li>
<p>Maroon=3D S4D medication - #800000</p></li>
</ol></li>
<li>
<p>Given the AIN has logged in, when they click on the Emergency Stock tab,=
 then error message appears, user should logout and login with RN/EN/Manage=
r to administer</p></li>
<li>
<p>If the facility disabled =E2=80=9CEnable Emergency Med administration fo=
r Enrolled Nurse=E2=80=9D, when EN has logged in and clicks on Emergency St=
ock tab, error message appears, user should logout and login with RN/Manage=
r to administer</p></li>
</ol>

<p><strong>Requirements</strong></p>
<ol start=3D"1">
<li>
<p>When the user selects NIM tab, then the NIM screen appears AND [(NIM)] w=
ill be displayed in the back button section after the date.</p></li>
<li>
<p>The following headings will appear:</p>
<ol start=3D"1">
<li>
<p>Medication</p>
<ol start=3D"1">
<li>
<p>Have an image of the medication on the left</p></li>
<li>
<p>Display either warning icon or tick icon- see below which one applies</p=
></li>
</ol></li>
<li>
<p>Medication name</p>
<ol start=3D"1">
<li>
<p>Below medication name display comments. Data is pulled from NIM Maintena=
nce.</p></li>
</ol></li>
<li>
<p>ROA</p>
<ol start=3D"1">
<li>
<p>Data is pulled from medication in BESTpack</p></li>
</ol></li>
<li>
<p>Indication</p>
<ol start=3D"1">
<li>
<p>Text box</p></li>
<li>
<p>Data is pulled from NIM Maintenance.</p></li>
</ol></li>
<li>
<p>Qty</p>
<ol start=3D"1">
<li>
<p>Text box</p></li>
</ol></li>
<li>
<p>Admin</p>
<ol start=3D"1">
<li>
<p>Check box</p></li>
</ol></li>
</ol></li>
<li>
<p>Given the facility is not set up with NIM, when the user clicks on the N=
IM tab, then they will see the header with no medication below.</p></li>
<li>
<p>Given the facility is set up with NIM, when the user clicks on the NIM t=
ab, then they will see the list of medications set up from BESTpack.</p></l=
i>
<li>
<p>For Phase 1, do not have any review process for NIM, will update it to n=
ext release=20
<del>Given the user has not been reviewed electronically for a medication, =
then</del></p>
<ol start=3D"1">
<li>
<p>
<del>The warning sign will be displayed next to the medication, AND</del></=
p></li>
<li>
<p>
<del>When the user attempts to administer the medication, then they will se=
e a warning in the modal will the following text: =E2=80=98Medications with=
 a =E2=80=93 have not been electronically reviewed by the prescriber for th=
is resent. Please refer to paper NIM List if available.=E2=80=99 AND</del><=
/p></li>
<li>
<p>
<del>The user will be able to press =E2=80=98Confirm=E2=80=99 on the Confir=
mation modal and administer the medication.</del></p></li>
</ol></li>
<li>
<p>If medication is Paracetamol, then hide =E2=80=98Check 24hr Usage=E2=80=
=99 button.</p></li>
<li>
<p>When there is a medication image available, display this in the space pr=
ovided</p></li>
<li>
<p>When there is no medication image available, display the default image (=
name: camera)</p></li>
<li>
<p>Given the facility has saved data in the =E2=80=98Indication=E2=80=99 se=
ction in NIM Maintenance, when the NIM tab loads, then they will see the da=
ta in the =E2=80=98Indication=E2=80=99 column.</p></li>
<li>
<p>Given the facility has not saved data in the =E2=80=98Indication=E2=80=
=99 section in NIM Maintenance, when the NIM tab loads, then they will see =
an empty text box in the =E2=80=98Indication=E2=80=99 column AND they can s=
ave data in the column. Is this necessary for MVP? Save to clinical system?=
</p></li>
<li>
<p>When the user administers the medication, then the confirmation modal po=
ps up.</p></li>
<li>
<p>Given the AIN has logged in, when they click on the NIM tab, then error =
message appears, user should logout and login with RN/EN to administer</p><=
/li>
<li>
<p>If the facility disabled =E2=80=9CEnable NIM administration for Enrolled=
 Nurse=E2=80=9D, when EN has logged in and clicks on NIM tab, error message=
 appears, user should logout and login with RN/Manager to administer</p></l=
i>

<p><strong>Requirements</strong></p>
<ol start=3D"1">
<li>
<p>When the user selects =E2=80=98Prog. Note=E2=80=99 tab, then the Progres=
s Note modal will appear</p></li>
<li>
<p>When the user enters text into the modal and clicks save, then the data =
is saved to a temporary table AND the data will appear in the =E2=80=98Prog=
ress Notes=E2=80=99 tab on home screen AND the modal closes</p></li>
<li>
<p>When the user selects the =E2=80=98Prog. Note=E2=80=99 tab AND they have=
 already entered data for that dose round whilst on the Dose Round Resident=
 Info screen, then when the Progress Note modal appears, it will be empty.<=
/p></li>
<li>
<p>When the modal appears and the user clicks cancel, then the modal will c=
lose AND any data in the modal will be deleted.</p></li>
